GFS Neohellenic Regular (GFSNeohellenic.ttf)

name

Mac NID 16/17

If NID 2 and 17 = 'Regular': Mac NID 16 should match NID 1.
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). This is true for MS Office Version 1639 and lower. Even though Microsoft has changed it with version 1640 (fast insider, June 2020) we keep this as an error, because most of the current MS Office users won't update in the near future. More infos here:
Cross Platform Issues

GFS Neohellenic Regular (GFSNeohellenic.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'GFSNeohellenic-Regular', Everything looks good.

Pass

GFS Neohellenic Bold (GFSNeohellenicBold.ttf)

name

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'GFSNeohellenic-Bold', Everything looks good.

Pass

GFS Neohellenic Bold (GFSNeohellenicBold.ttf)

name

Mac NID 16/17

Mac NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'GFS Neohellenic' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Bold' = NID 1 'GFS Neohellenic' + 'Space' + NID 2 'Bold'.

Pass

GFS Neohellenic Bold (GFSNeohellenicBold.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'GFSNeohellenic-Bold', Everything looks good.

Pass

GFS Neohellenic Bold (GFSNeohellenicBold.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'GFS Neohellenic' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Bold' = NID 1 'GFS Neohellenic' + 'Space' + NID 2 'Bold'.

Pass

NID 6 is 'GFSNeohellenic-BoldItalic', Everything looks good.

GFS Neohellenic Bold Italic (GFSNeohellenicBoldItalic.ttf)

name

Mac NID 16/17

Mac NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'GFS Neohellenic' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Bold Italic' = NID 1 'GFS Neohellenic' + 'Space' + NID 2 'Bold Italic'.

Pass
